< review>
I always enjoy the opportunity to have some GK Mongolian BBQ bowl. I have ate at most of them in the valley from Stockton to Manteca to Tracy. This one unfortunately lacks leadership. I know it opened not long before Covid but the customer service is just not there yet. This past visit one of the guys left the grill to stand at the end of the counter and talk for about 20 minutes to a girl he knew. It left one guy on the grill and slowed down the whole process. The time before that we could not get a drink refill to save our lives. When I Grubhub it in a few weeks ago it tasted like that added Lobster sauce which I hate and I was not able to eat it. This location needs some TLC to get up to par with the rest of the GK's.< /review>

< text>
Super pretty trail with a nice view both up and down. It's an out and back so you can make it as short as you want. There are a lot of spots to stop and rest along the way and just take in the beautiful view.

It's a pretty easy hike. There's a steady incline on the way up and going down is quick and easy.

There's a free parking lot right at the head of the trail and some street parking if the lot is full. I came on a Saturday afternoon and there were still several spots when I arrived and the lot was almost empty when I left.<//text>

<Review>AJEET is best barber in town I bring my kids for Mundan , Ajeet who did the shaving of hair or known as the Mundan or Mottai in India. When I decided to do the mottai thing, my husband, my mom, and many others were not sure about the need or how we would find someone here in the US. I really wanted to keep the tradition and avoid doing it in India at all costs cuz i could not stomach the hygiene factor. Though the temples offered a mundane service, it was not a proper tonsure like they do in India. Thanks to my fellow Indians who subjected their poor children as well, I found Ajeet Mundan & Barber Shop and we walked away happy customers. Ajeet was really friendly and super sweet to accommodate us even though we were late. He did an excellent job and I felt it was a better mundan than ones done in India. He is super patient with the babies and takes his time to be extra careful and thorough.

It is a shop for kids mundan in fremont and it gets very busy quickly. This seems to be the spot to go if you are looking to do a proper mundan. With that said, the barbers are nice and the place is relatively clean. NoTE-This is perfect shop they have a kids cartoon character on wall it‚Äôs look great

Here are some good tidbits to consider:

1. Prepare and plan. You will definitely need two people other than the barber himself. It depends on your kid. Usually mine is Dennis the menace but we were lucky to see the baby go before us to know what to do and what not to do.

2. Make an appointment. If you are going by auspicious times (like my mom forced me to) Ajeet was nice enough to offer to come in at opening but we could not make that time. When we got there, there were already 3 people waiting for him including a baby and it was only 9 am. BE ON TIME and aim for a day that you can get an appointment.

3. Take distractions like an iPhone or iPad (ask for the wifi ahead of you sitting in chair), a friendly grandmother, a clown, whatever to help keep your child distracted.

4. Wear clothes that you don't care if hair gets on them. The baby that went before us had a melt down just at the start of the cover Ajeet tried to put on the mom. Forget covering the kid- its not worth it.

5. Process: first ajeet will buzz off the hair with an electric buzz- it will get to pretty close shave. Then he wets the head slightly and then goes over the head with a sterilized straight razor.

6. Brace yourself. Decide who is going to hold the child. It is best to get someone who the child has best temperament and one other person to hold head (more like put it on lock down) if needed.

My son who was 17 months old surprisingly didn't fuss much, to my surprise. The baby before us screamed for mercy- so again it depends on your child. During the straight blade part, Ajeet suggested not to hold head to see how he reacts and honestly he just sat watching Moana (for the 10935935 time

7. Once Ajeet is done with the straight razor, he put powder on the head and covered any missing spots. bring a large zip lock bag if you want to take it back to donate to the temple, etc.

9. We changed our son and wiped him down in our car. I brought a big sheet to catch any hair that may fall. It took him some time and he was missing his long hair

*bring cash- if you use CC- then its Extra $ charge*

Don‚Äôt Fear,You're in great hands!< /Review>< response>

< review>
2 spicy Tonkatsu ramens, one with chicken and one with pork belly. This place has the best ramen I've had in a restaurant. Every restaurant I've been to had bland ramen, but sake sushi hits those taste buds.
I've had the shuyo and miso ramen as well, but It has been a while.
The pork belly is tender, with a bit of fat on it; it has a really good flavor to it. The chicken has no flavor but its still good with the broth. The noodles are PERFECT, not aw mushy, they are a perfect al dente. Overall this place always hits the spot, even on a hot day lol.
If you like ramen and find it hard to find a really good ramen place, THIS place can definitely fill the craving.< /review>
